By Leen Randell

Updated: Feb 22, 2025

The Polypodiaceae Family

The polypodiaceae rank is a family of plants, specifically referring to the family of ferns commonly known as the polypody fern family.

This family consists of about 1,000 species of ferns, which are typically found in tropical and subtropical regions around the world. The polypodiaceae family is characterized by its diverse range of species, varying in size, shape, and leaf structure.

Many species within this family are epiphytes, growing on other plants for support, while others are terrestrial or rock-dwelling.
